/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[lastpayment]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:17 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[lastpayment](
@booking_id INT,
@room INT) 
RETURNS @lastpayment TABLE (
	payment_id		bigint		NULL,
	booking_id		bigint		NULL,
	reservasi_id	bigint		NULL,
	jumlahpayment	bigint		NULL,
	tggalpayment	datetime	NULL,
	RoomNo			int			NULL
) 
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT @lastpayment

select *
from(
select p.payment_id,p.booking_id,p.reservasi_id,p.jumlahpayment,p.tggalpayment, r.kamar_no as 'RoomNo'
from pembayaran p
inner join 
Reservasi r
on r.reservasi_id = p.reservasi_id
inner join
Booking b
on b.booking_id = r.booking_id and b.booking_id = @booking_id
and convert(varchar,p.tggalpayment,101)+' '+convert(varchar,datepart(hh,p.tggalpayment))+':'+right('0'+convert(varchar,datepart(mi,p.tggalpayment)),2) = (
select convert(varchar,max(tggalpayment),101)+' '+convert(varchar,datepart(hh,max(tggalpayment)))+':'+right('0'+convert(varchar,datepart(mi,max(tggalpayment))),2) from pembayaran where booking_id=@booking_id)
) a
where
case when @room is null then 1 else [RoomNo] end
=
case when @room is null then 1 else @room end
	RETURN
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_generate_harga]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[sp_generate_harga]
as
begin

----hapus tabel harga
truncate table harga

insert into harga
----Hitung fluktuasi harga periodik----
select
p.tanggal_id,p.kamar_tipe_id
,case when k.harga is not null then k.harga else p.harga end harga
,case when k.harga_weekend is not null then k.harga_weekend else p.harga_weekend end harga_weekend
from 
(
    select
    tanggal_id,kamar_tipe_id,harga,harga_weekend
    from 
    (
        SELECT 
        *
        ,ROW_NUMBER() over(partition by tanggal_id,kamar_tipe_id order by tgl_berlaku desc) urutan
        FROM 
        [dbo].[Tanggal] t
        left join 
        dbo.Harga_Periodik 
        hp
        on t.tanggal_id >= hp.tgl_berlaku 
    )a
    where urutan = 1

----Hitung fluktuasi harga periodik----
)p
left join 
----Hitung fluktuasi harga khusus----
dbo.Harga_Khusus k
on p.tanggal_id>=k.tgl_berlaku and p.tanggal_id <=k.tgl_berakhir and k.kamar_tipe_id=p.kamar_tipe_id
----Hitung fluktuasi harga khusus----
----Test Harga Khusus----
--where day(tanggal_id) between 23 and 27 and MONTH(tanggal_id) = 12
----Test Harga Khusus----
order by tanggal_id

delete from harga where harga is null

end
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[infoPembayaran]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[infoPembayaran](
@booking_id INT,
@room INT)
RETURNS @infoPembayaran TABLE (
	payment_id		bigint		NULL,
	booking_id		bigint		NULL,
	reservasi_id	bigint		NULL,
	payment			varchar(50)	NULL,
	nopayment		varchar(50)	NULL,
	jumlahpayment	bigint		NULL,
	tggalpayment	datetime	NULL,
	staff_id		int			NULL,
	NoPemesanan		bigint		NULL,
	RoomNo			int			NULL,
	Status			varchar(50)	NULL
) 
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT @infoPembayaran
		select *
		from(
		select p.*, r.kamar_no as 'RoomNo', r.status 'Status'
		from pembayaran p
		inner join 
		Reservasi r
		on r.reservasi_id = p.reservasi_id
		inner join
		Booking b
		on b.booking_id = r.booking_id and b.booking_id = @booking_id
		) a
		where
		case when @room is null then 1 else [RoomNo] end
		=
		case when @room is null then 1 else @room end
	RETURN
END;
GO

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[infoReservasi_pre09052014]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[infoReservasi_pre09052014](
@booking_id INT,
@room INT)
RETURNS @infoReservasi TABLE (
   Datee		datetime		NULL,
   RoomNo		int				NULL,
   RoomType		varchar(30)     NULL,
   Descriptionn varchar(MAX)	NULL,
   Charges		int				NULL,
   urut_tampil	int				NULL,
   harga		int				NULL,
   biayadiskon	int				NULL
) 
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT @infoReservasi
		select
		*
		from
		(
			select 
			convert(date,tgl.tanggal_id) as 'Datee'
			,r.kamar_no as 'RoomNo'--tamu,alamat,kota,min(r.checkin) checkin,max(r.checkout) checkout
			,kt.kamar_tipe as 'RoomType'
			,'Room Charge (' + isnull(t.sebutan,'') + ' ' + isnull(t.gelar,'') + ' ' + t.tamu + ')' as 'Descriptionn'
			, case when DATENAME(dw,tgl.tanggal_id) in ('Saturday','Sunday') then h.harga_weekend else h.harga end Charges
		--	,downpayment
			,1 urut_tampil
			,bd.harga
			,bd.harga*case when DATENAME(dw,tgl.tanggal_id) in ('Saturday','Sunday') then h.harga_weekend else h.harga end as 'biayadiskon'
			from 
			Booking b
			inner join
			Booking_Diskon bd
			on bd.booking_diskon_id=b.booking_diskon_id
			inner join 
			Tamu t
			on b.tamu_id = t.tamu_id
			inner join 
			Reservasi r
			on b.booking_id = r.booking_id
			inner join 
			Tanggal tgl
			on convert(date,tgl.tanggal_id) >= convert(date,r.checkin) and convert(date,tgl.tanggal_id) < convert(date,r.realcheckout)
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join 
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			inner join 
			Harga h
			on 
			h.kamar_tipe_id = k.kamar_tipe_id
			and h.tanggal_id = tgl.tanggal_id
			where 
			b.booking_id = @booking_id
		--	and 
		--	r.reservasi_id = @reservasi_id
			--group by tamu,alamat,kota
			union

			select 
			min(convert(date,checkin))
			,r.kamar_no
			,kamar_tipe
			,'Down Payment'
			,sum(downpayment)*-1
			,0
			,1
			,sum(downpayment)*-1
			from 
			Reservasi r
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			where 
			booking_id = @booking_id
			group by 
			r.kamar_no
			,kamar_tipe
			having sum(downpayment) > 0
			union
			select r.checkout 'Date' ,r.kamar_no as 'Room No'
			,kt.kamar_tipe as 'Room Type'
				,'Restaurant' as 'Description'
				,r.tag_restoran Charges
				,2
				,1
				,r.tag_restoran
				from 
			Reservasi r
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join 
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			where r.booking_id=@booking_id

			union

			select 
			max(convert(date,t.tanggal_id)) 'Date'
			,r.kamar_no
			,kt.kamar_tipe
			,'Transport'
			,sum(r.tag_transport) Charges
		--	,0
			,3
			,1
			,sum(r.tag_transport)
			from 
			Reservasi r
			inner join
			Tanggal t
			on
			t.tanggal_id between r.checkin and r.realcheckout
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join 
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			where 
			r.booking_id = @booking_id
			group by 
			r.kamar_no
			,kt.kamar_tipe
			having sum(tag_transport) > 0
		)a
		where
		case when @room is null then 1 else [RoomNo] end
		=
		case when @room is null then 1 else @room end
		order by a.Datee,urut_tampil,[RoomNo]
	RETURN
END;
GO

CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[infoReservasi](
@booking_id INT,

RETURNS @infoReservasi TABLE (
   Datee		datetime		NULL,
   RoomNo		int				NULL,
   RoomType		varchar(30)     NULL,
   Descriptionn varchar(MAX)	NULL,
   Charges		int				NULL,
   urut_tampil	int				NULL,
   harga		int				NULL,
   biayadiskon	int				NULL
) 
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT @infoReservasi
		select
		*
		from
		(
			select 
			convert(date,tgl.tanggal_id) as 'Datee'
			,r.kamar_no as 'RoomNo'--tamu,alamat,kota,min(r.checkin) checkin,max(r.checkout) checkout
			,kt.kamar_tipe as 'RoomType'
			,'Room Charge (' + isnull(t.sebutan,'') + ' ' + isnull(t.gelar,'') + ' ' + t.tamu + ')' as 'Descriptionn'
			, case when DATENAME(dw,tgl.tanggal_id) in ('Saturday','Sunday') then h.harga_weekend else h.harga end Charges
		--	,downpayment
			,1 urut_tampil
			,bd.harga
			,bd.harga*case when DATENAME(dw,tgl.tanggal_id) in ('Saturday','Sunday') then h.harga_weekend else h.harga end as 'biayadiskon'
			from 
			Booking b
			inner join
			Booking_Diskon bd
			on bd.booking_diskon_id=b.booking_diskon_id
			
			inner join 
			Reservasi r
			on b.booking_id = r.booking_id
			inner join 
			Tamu t
			on r.tamu_id = t.tamu_id
			inner join 
			Tanggal tgl
			on convert(date,tgl.tanggal_id) >= convert(date,r.checkin) and convert(date,tgl.tanggal_id) < convert(date,r.realcheckout)
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join 
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			inner join 
			Harga h
			on 
			h.kamar_tipe_id = k.kamar_tipe_id
			and h.tanggal_id = tgl.tanggal_id
			where 
			b.booking_id = @booking_id
		--	and 
		--	r.reservasi_id = @reservasi_id
			--group by tamu,alamat,kota
			union

			select 
			min(convert(date,checkin))
			,r.kamar_no
			,kamar_tipe
			,'Down Payment'
			,sum(downpayment)*-1
			,0
			,1
			,sum(downpayment)*-1
			from 
			Reservasi r
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			where 
			booking_id = @booking_id
			group by 
			r.kamar_no
			,kamar_tipe
			having sum(downpayment) > 0
			union
			select r.checkout 'Date' ,r.kamar_no as 'Room No'
			,kt.kamar_tipe as 'Room Type'
				,'Restaurant' as 'Description'
				,r.tag_restoran Charges
				,2
				,1
				,r.tag_restoran
				from 
			Reservasi r
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join 
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			where r.booking_id=@booking_id

			union

			select 
			max(convert(date,t.tanggal_id)) 'Date'
			,r.kamar_no
			,kt.kamar_tipe
			,'Transport'
			,sum(r.tag_transport) Charges
		--	,0
			,3
			,1
			,sum(r.tag_transport)
			from 
			Reservasi r
			inner join
			Tanggal t
			on
			t.tanggal_id between r.checkin and r.realcheckout
			inner join 
			Kamar k
			on 
			r.kamar_no = k.kamar_no
			inner join 
			Kamar_Tipe kt
			on k.kamar_tipe_id = kt.kamar_tipe_id
			where 
			r.booking_id = @booking_id
			group by 
			r.kamar_no
			,kt.kamar_tipe
			having sum(tag_transport) > 0
		)a
		where
		case when @room is null then 1 else [RoomNo] end
		=
		case when @room is null then 1 else @room end
		order by a.Datee,urut_tampil,[RoomNo]
	RETURN
END;

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[infoPemesanan]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[infoPemesanan](
@booking_id INT,
@room INT)
RETURNS @infoPemesanan TABLE (
	pemesanan_id	bigint,
   TanggalPesan		datetime	NULL,
   Jenis		varchar(50)		NULL,
   Harga		int				NULL,
   RoomNo		int				NULL
) 
AS
BEGIN
	INSERT @infoPemesanan
		select * 
		from (
		select p.pemesanan_id, p.tgl_pemesanan as 'TanggalPesan' ,it.item_tipe as 'Jenis' ,p.harga as 'Harga' ,r.kamar_no as 'RoomNo'
		from 
		Pemesanan p
		inner join
		Reservasi r
		on p.reservasi_id = r.reservasi_id
		inner join 
		Booking b
		on r.booking_id=@booking_id 
		inner join 
		Item i 
		on i.item_id = p.item_id
		inner join
		Item_Tipe it
		on it.item_tipe_id = i.item_tipe_id
		group by
		p.pemesanan_id, p.tgl_pemesanan,it.item_tipe,p.harga,r.kamar_no
		)a
		where
		case when @room is null then 1 else [RoomNo] end
		=
		case when @room is null then 1 else @room end
	RETURN
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[NewSelectPembayaran]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[NewSelectPembayaran]
(
	@booking_id int,
	@room int
)
AS
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
SELECT        payment_id, booking_id, reservasi_id, payment, nopayment, jumlahpayment, tggalpayment, staff_id, NoPemesanan, RoomNo, Status
FROM            dbo.infoPembayaran(@booking_id, @room) AS infoPembayaran_1
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[NewSelectLastPayment]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[NewSelectLastPayment]
(
	@booking_id int,
	@room int
)
AS
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
SELECT        *
FROM            dbo.lastpayment(@booking_id, @room) AS LastPayment
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[NewSelectCommand]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[NewSelectCommand]
(
	@booking_id int,
	@room int
)
AS
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
SELECT        Datee, RoomNo, RoomType, Descriptionn, Charges, urut_tampil, harga, biayadiskon
FROM            dbo.infoReservasi(@booking_id, @room) AS infoReservasi_1
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

(
	@booking_id int,
	@room int
)
AS
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[NewSelectPemesanan]    Script Date: 11/24/2014 14:08:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[NewSelectPemesanan]
(
	@booking_id int,
	@room int
)
AS
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
SELECT        TanggalPesan, Jenis, Harga, RoomNo
FROM            dbo.infoPemesanan(@booking_id, @room) AS infoPemesanan_1
GO
